A key structural requirement: the candidate must contain an \(A^{c}\) (or \(|A|^c\)) power term with a free exponent so we can set it to \(1/3\). Most candidates only have \(A^2\) and \(A\exp(\cdot)\) and rational-in-\(t\) extras, so they cannot generate \(A^{1/3}\).

With A≥0, |A|^c8 = A^c8. Set c8=1/3 to get A^(1/3). But we need A*exp(αt), not just exp(αt). The exponential terms don't have A dependence. Missing A*exp(αt).
